RichDad-1405 :: So what causes the confusion? Or how could something so simple be so screwed up? Why would someone buy an asset that was really a liability. [sound:TR02-1405.mp3] ;RichDad-1405 :: xxx
RichDad-1406 :: The answer is found in basic education. [sound:TR02-1406.mp3] ;RichDad-1406 :: xxx
RichDad-1407 :: We focus on the word “literacy” and not “financial literacy. [sound:TR02-1407.mp3] ;RichDad-1407 :: xxx
RichDad-1408 :: ” What defines something to be an asset, or something to be a liability are not words. [sound:TR02-1408.mp3] ;RichDad-1408 :: xxx
RichDad-1409 :: In fact, if you really want to be confused, look up the words “asset” and “liability” in the dictionary. [sound:TR02-1409.mp3] ;RichDad-1409 :: xxx
RichDad-1410 :: I know the definition may sound good to a trained accountant, but for the average person it makes no sense. [sound:TR02-1410.mp3] ;RichDad-1410 :: xxx
RichDad-1411 :: But we adults are often too proud to admit that something does not make sense. [sound:TR02-1411.mp3] ;RichDad-1411 :: xxx

RichDad-1414 :: ” “In accounting,” rich dad would say, it's not the numbers, but what the numbers are telling you. [sound:TR02-1414.mp3] ;RichDad-1414 :: xxx
RichDad-1415 :: It's just like words. [sound:TR02-1415.mp3] ;RichDad-1415 :: xxx

RichDad-1420 :: For example, I recently bought a new VCR It came with an instruction book that explained how to program the VCR All I wanted to do was record my favorite TV show on Friday night. [sound:TR02-1420.mp3] ;RichDad-1420 :: xxx

RichDad-1423 :: I get an “A” for recognizing the words. [sound:TR02-1423.mp3] ;RichDad-1423 :: xxx

RichDad-1425 :: And so it is with financial statements for most people. [sound:TR02-1425.mp3] ;RichDad-1425 :: xxx
RichDad-1426 :: “If you want to be rich, you've got to read and understand numbers. [sound:TR02-1426.mp3] ;RichDad-1426 :: xxx

RichDad-1709 :: Actually I borrowed it from a man named Buckminster Fuller Some call him a quack, and others call him a living genius. [sound:TR02-1709.mp3] ;RichDad-1709 :: xxx

RichDad-1713 :: or if I stopped working today, how long could I survive? Unlike net worth:the difference between your assets and liabilities, which is often filled with a person's expensive junk and opinions of what things are worth:this definition creates the possibility for developing a truly accurate measurement. [sound:TR02-1713.mp3] ;RichDad-1713 :: xxx
RichDad-1714 :: I could now measure and really know where I was in terms of my goal to become financially independent. [sound:TR02-1714.mp3] ;RichDad-1714 :: xxx

RichDad-1716 :: Wealth is the measure of the cash flow from the asset column compared with the expense column. [sound:TR02-1716.mp3] ;RichDad-1716 :: xxx
RichDad-1717 :: Let's use an example. [sound:TR02-1717.mp3] ;RichDad-1717 :: xxx
RichDad-1718 :: Let's say I have cash flow from my asset column of S J,000 a month. [sound:TR02-1718.mp3] ;RichDad-1718 :: xxx
RichDad-1719 :: And I have monthly expenses of 52,000. [sound:TR02-1719.mp3] ;RichDad-1719 :: xxx

RichDad-1733 :: And as long as I keep my expenses less than the cash flow from these assets, I will grow richer, with more and more income from sources other than my physical labor As this reinvestment process continues, I am well on my way to being rich. [sound:TR02-1733.mp3] ;RichDad-1733 :: xxx
